Hello folks,

    This is my suggested split for the OSX installers 2 packages, and a
few files to remove.

Miguel
-------------- next part --------------
Notes:

	Some glue static libraries are completely eliminated
	
	2.1 profile is not bundled with the runtime as it is useless
	on MacOS

	There are three sections in this file:

	RUNTIME:
	DELETE: Eliminate from the distribution:
	SDK: Goes into the SDK

RUNTIME:
